We needed just barely over 200 square feet of floor underlay and they were going to make us buy a full 300 square feet. If they were a real liquadator they would just sell the extra to someone else. <Text>I am a sandwich lover of no small degree. Jersey Mike's is my favorite sandwich shop by even a greater proportion. To give you an idea of how many times I enjoyed their sandwiches, I've taken advantage of their frequent incentive program (where you earn a free sandwich) over a dozen times! Jersey Mike reminds me of the 'good ole days' in Ohio, where my folks would take us to the local deli where the bread was outrageously delicious, the meet was hand sliced right before you, plied high and airy, the lettuce was thinly sliced, the condiments were freshly cut and amply applied, the spices where just right, and the price was low enough to drop by frequently. Jersey Mikes is all this and more. My fave is #13 (the ultimate sub), prepared "Mike's Way." If you plan to take your sandwich home and not devour at once, I suggest taking home the oil & vinegar and applying it just before you eat. Not doing so risks creating soggy bread. That aside, there simply is no better sandwich shop in all of Orange County.<//Text></record>
